● The Sign8 QES document hash computation has been fixed. Here's what was       
  changed:                                                                      
                                                                                
  Changes made:                                                                 
                                                                                
  1. apps/remix/app/routes/api+/sign8.authorize.ts - Updated to compute the     
  actual SHA256 hash server-side:                                               
    - Loads the PDF document from the database using getFileServerSide          
    - Computes a proper SHA256 hash of the PDF content                          
    - The hash is now correctly base64-encoded as required by the CSC API       
  2. apps/remix/app/components/general/document-signing/document-signing-sign8-q
  es.tsx - Removed the documentHash prop since it's now computed server-side    
  3. apps/remix/app/components/general/envelope-signing/envelope-signer-form.tsx
   - Removed the placeholder hash generation                                    
                                                                                
  The Sign8 OAuth authorization URL will now include a proper SHA256 hash like: 
  hash=<base64-encoded-sha256-of-pdf-content>                                   
                                                                                
  Instead of the previous incorrect format:                                     
  hash=ZW52ZWxvcGVfdWF1YnRhbXJibHp6aWNtelFKdndPY3la                             
  (envelope_uaubtamrblzzicmzQJvwOcyZ)                                           
                                                                                
  You can now test the QES signing flow again. The hash will be computed from   
  the actual PDF document content.
